$YP(document).ready(function() {
	$YP('#ypgBody .ypgDealsText')
	.hover(
		function() {
			$YP(this).css('cursor', 'pointer');
			$YP(this).find('span').css('text-decoration', 'underline');
		},
		function() {
			$YP(this).css('cursor', 'auto');
			$YP(this).find('span').css('text-decoration', 'none');
		}
	)
	.click(function(event) {
		//console.log($YP(this).find('a'));
		//console.dir(event.target);

		// Idea: by clicking div, act as if user had clicked the anchor nested inside.  Can't because cause infinite loop.
		// Programatically clicking on nested anchor triggers this handler again and ...again!!!
		//$YP(this).find('a').trigger('click'); // this will cause infinite loop

		// Use of .triggerHandler does not bubble event up like .trigger 
		//$YP(this).find('a').triggerHandler('click'); // doesn't trigger following href and doesn't trigger code attached to mousedown attribute 

		// If user clicks on anchor directly no need to do following as it will send a duplicate analytics event.
		if(event.target.tagName == "DIV") {
			// This triggers the analytics info to be sent.
			$YP(this).find('a').triggerHandler('mousedown'); //doesn't trigger following href but it does trigger code atttached to mousedown attribute

			// Use this to follow the link of the anchor
			document.location.href = $YP(this).find('a').first().attr('href');
		}
	});
});

	var showPhotoPanel = function(listingIndex) {
		var jComments = $YP( "#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex ).comments();
		if(jComments.length) {
			$YP( "#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex).html( jComments.html() );
			$YP('#StartHiddenPhotoSection_' + listingIndex + ' .photoControls').jCarouselLite({
				btnNext: "#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlNext",
				btnPrev: "#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlPrev",
       			vertical: true,
       			circular: false,
       			speed: 1000,
       			beforeStart: function() {
    			},
   				afterEnd: function() {
   					if ($YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlPrev").hasClass("disabled")) { $YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlPrev").html("&nbsp;"); };
   					if ($YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlNext").hasClass("disabled")) { $YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlNext").html("&nbsp;"); };
   					if (!$YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlPrev").hasClass("disabled")) { $YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlPrev").html(" &lt;&lt; "); };
   					if (!$YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlNext").hasClass("disabled")) { $YP("#StartHiddenPhotoSection_" + listingIndex + " .photoControlNext").html(" &gt;&gt; "); };
    			}
			});
		}
	}

	var showVideoPanel = function(listingIndex) {
		var videoProfileId = $YP( "#videoProfileIdValue_" + listingIndex ).text();
		if(videoProfileId) {
			var videos = '';
			videos = $YP('#VideoSectionTemplate').html();
			videos = videos.replace(/PROFILEID_2B_OVERRIDDEN/g, videoProfileId);
			var myExperienceId = 'myExperience_' + listingIndex;
			videos = videos.replace(/PLAYERID_2B_OVERRIDDEN/g, myExperienceId);

			$YP('#inlineVideoHolder_' + listingIndex).html(videos);

var toggle_headingMode = function() {
	var mode = "print";
	var url = window.location.href;
	var pname = 'headingMode=';
	if (url.indexOf(pname) == -1) {
		url += (url.indexOf('?') == -1 ? '?' : '&') + pname + mode;
	} else {
		url = url.replace(/headingMode=(web|print)/i, pname + mode);
	}
	window.location.href = url;
}

	var sendPageViewAnalytics = function(utag_values) {
		if (typeof utag_values == 'undefined')
			setAnalytics();
		else
			utag_data = $YP.extend(utag_data, utag_values);
	
		utag_data.pv_ssologged = '';

		if(typeof ypgYidManager !== 'undefined') {
			if(ypgYidManager.isLoggedIn()) {
				utag_data.pv_ssologged = '1';
			}			
		}

		if(typeof YPG.LOC != 'undefined') {
			utag_data.prod_imp = YPG.LOC.prod_imp;
		}
